<div class="endpoint"><div class="section-left"><div><span class="endpoint-text"><span class="endpoint-method endpoint-method-post">post</span>&nbsp;<span class="endpoint-path">https://api.openai.com/v1/chat/completions</span></span></div><div class="docs-markdown-content endpoint-summary"><p><strong>Starting a new project?</strong> We recommend trying <a href="/docs/api-reference/responses" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">Responses</a>
to take advantage of the latest OpenAI platform features. Compare
<a href="/docs/guides/responses-vs-chat-completions?api-mode=responses" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">Chat Completions with Responses</a>.</p>
<hr>
<p>Creates a model response for the given chat conversation. Learn more in the
<a href="/docs/guides/text-generation" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">text generation</a>, <a href="/docs/guides/vision" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">vision</a>,
and <a href="/docs/guides/audio" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">audio</a> guides.</p>
<p>Parameter support can differ depending on the model used to generate the
response, particularly for newer reasoning models. Parameters that are only
supported for reasoning models are noted below. For the current state of
unsupported parameters in reasoning models,
<a href="/docs/guides/reasoning" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">refer to the reasoning guide</a>.</p></div><div class="param-section"><h4>Request body</h4><div class="param-table" class="param-depr">Deprecated</div><div class="param-type"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>string or object</p></div></div><div class="param-optl">Optional</div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>Deprecated in favor of <code>tool_choice</code>.</p>
<p>Controls which (if any) function is called by the model.</p>
<p><code>none</code> means the model will not call a function and instead generates a
message.</p>
<p><code>auto</code> means the model can pick between generating a message or calling a
function.</p>
<p>Specifying a particular function via <code>{"name": "my_function"}</code> forces the
model to call that function.</p>
<p><code>none</code> is the default when no functions are present. <code>auto</code> is the default
if functions are present.</p></div></div><button class="param-expand-button" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="chat_create-function_call_table"><span class="param-expand-chevron" aria-hidden="true"><svg width="1em" height="1em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4.293 8.293a1 1 0 0 1 1.414 0L12 14.586l6.293-6.293a1 1 0 1 1 1.414 1.414l-7 7a1 1 0 0 1-1.414 0l-7-7a1 1 0 0 1 0-1.414Z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></span><span>Show possible types</span></button></div><div class="param-row" id="chat_create-functions" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a><div class="param-name">logit_bias</div><div class="param-type"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>map</p></div></div><div class="param-optl">Optional</div><div class="param-default">Defaults to null</div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>Modify the likelihood of specified tokens appearing in the completion.</p>
<p>Accepts a JSON object that maps tokens (specified by their token ID in the
tokenizer) to an associated bias value from -100 to 100. Mathematically,
the bias is added to the logits generated by the model prior to sampling.
The exact effect will vary per model, but values between -1 and 1 should
decrease or increase likelihood of selection; values like -100 or 100
should result in a ban or exclusive selection of the relevant token.</p></div></div></div><div class="param-row" id="chat_create-logprobs" data-normalized-id="chat-create-logprobs"><div class="param-row-header api-ref-anchor-link-hover"><a href="#chat_create-logprobs" data-anchor="chat_create-logprobs" id="chat_create-logprobs-anchor" data-normalized-id="chat-create-logprobs-anchor" class="docs-markdown-content"><p>boolean or null</p></div></div><div class="param-optl">Optional</div><div class="param-default">Defaults to false</div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>Whether to return log probabilities of the output tokens or not. If true,
returns the log probabilities of each output token returned in the
<code>content</code> of <code>message</code>.</p></div></div></div><div class="param-row" id="chat_create-max_completion_tokens" data-normalized-id="chat-create-max-completion-tokens"><div class="param-name">metadata</div><div class="param-type"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>map</p></div></div><div class="param-optl">Optional</div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>Set of 16 key-value pairs that can be attached to an object. useful for storing additional information about the object in a structured
format, and querying for objects via API or the dashboard.</p>

with a maximum length of 512 characters.</p></div></div></div><div class="param-row" id="chat_create-modalities" data-normalized-id="chat-create-modalities"><div class="param-row-header api-ref-anchor-link-hover"><a href="#chat_create-modalities" data-anchor="chat_create-modalities" id="chat_create-modalities-anchor" data-normalized-id="chat-create-modalities-anchor" class="api-ref-anchor-link"><svg width="1em" height="1em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor"><path d="M18.2929 5.7071C16.4743 3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 11.7071 5.7071L10.7071 6.7071C10.3166 7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 9.29289 6.7071C8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 5.68341 9.29289 5.29289L10.2929 4.29289C12.8926 1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 19.7071 4.29289C22.3068 6.89255 22.3068 11.1074 19.7071 13.7071L18.7071 14.7071C18.3166 15.0976 17.6834 15.0976 17.2929 14.7071C16.9024 14.3166 16.9024 13.6834 17.2929 13.2929L18.2929 12.2929C20.1115 10.4743 20.1115 7.52572 18.2929 5.7071ZM15.7071 8.29289C16.0976 8.68341 16.0976 9.31658 15.7071 9.7071L9.7071 15.7071C9.31658 16.0976 8.68341 16.0976 8.29289 15.7071C7.90236 15.3166 7.90236 14.6834 8.29289 14.2929L14.2929 8.29289C14.6834 7.90236 15.3166 7.90236 15.7071 8.29289ZM6.7071 9.29289C7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 10.3166 6.7071 10.7071L5.7071 11.7071C3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 16.4743 5.7071 18.2929C7.52572 20.1115 10.4743 20.1115 12.2929 18.2929L13.2929 17.2929C13.6834 16.9024 14.3166 16.9024 14.7071 17.2929C15.0976 17.6834 15.0976 18.3166 14.7071 18.7071L13.7071 19.7071C11.1074 22.3068 6.89255 22.3068 4.29289 19.7071C1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 12.8926 4.29289 10.2929L5.29289 9.29289C5.68341 8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 6.7071 9.29289Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a><div class="param-name">modalities</div><div class="param-type"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>array</p></div></div><div class="param-optl">Optional</div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>Output types that you would like the model to generate.
Most models are capable of generating text, which is the default:</p>
<p><code>["text"]</code></p>
<p>The <code>gpt-4o-audio-preview</code> model can also be used to
<a href="/docs/guides/audio" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">generate audio</a>. To request that this model generate
both text and audio responses, you can use:</p>
<p><code>["text", "audio"]</code></p></div></div></div><div class="param-row" id="chat_create-n" data-normalized-id="chat-create-n"><div class="param-row-header api-ref-anchor-link-hover"><a href="#chat_create-n" data-anchor="chat_create-n" id="chat_create-n-anchor" data-normalized-id="chat-create-n-anchor" class="api-ref-anchor-link"><svg width="1em" height="1em" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor"><path d="M18.2929 5.7071C16.4743 3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 11.7071 5.7071L10.7071 6.7071C10.3166 7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 9.29289 6.7071C8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 5.68341 9.29289 5.29289L10.2929 4.29289C12.8926 1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 19.7071 4.29289C22.3068 6.89255 22.3068 11.1074 19.7071 13.7071L18.7071 14.7071C18.3166 15.0976 17.6834 15.0976 17.2929 14.7071C16.9024 14.3166 16.9024 13.6834 17.2929 13.2929L18.2929 12.2929C20.1115 10.4743 20.1115 7.52572 18.2929 5.7071ZM15.7071 8.29289C16.0976 8.68341 16.0976 9.31658 15.7071 9.7071L9.7071 15.7071C9.31658 16.0976 8.68341 16.0976 8.29289 15.7071C7.90236 15.3166 7.90236 14.6834 8.29289 14.2929L14.2929 8.29289C14.6834 7.90236 15.3166 7.90236 15.7071 8.29289ZM6.7071 9.29289C7.09763 9.68341 7.09763 10.3166 6.7071 10.7071L5.7071 11.7071C3.88849 13.5257 3.88849 16.4743 5.7071 18.2929C7.52572 20.1115 10.4743 20.1115 12.2929 18.2929L13.2929 17.2929C13.6834 16.9024 14.3166 16.9024 14.7071 17.2929C15.0976 17.6834 15.0976 18.3166 14.7071 18.7071L13.7071 19.7071C11.1074 22.3068 6.89255 22.3068 4.29289 19.7071C1.69322 17.1074 1.69322 12.8926 4.29289 10.2929L5.29289 9.29289C5.68341 8.90236 6.31658 8.90236 6.7071 9.29289Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a><div class="param-name">n</div><div class="param-type"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>integer or null</p></div></div><div class="param-optl">Optional</div><div class="param-default">Defaults to 1</div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>How many chat completion choices to generate for each input message. Note that you will be charged based on the number of generated tokens across all of the choices. Keep <code>n</code> as <code>1</code> to minimize costs.</p></div></div></div><div class="param-row" id="chat_create-parallel_tool_calls" data-normalized-id="chat-create-parallel-tool-calls"><div class="param-row-header api-ref-anchor-link-hover"><a href="#chat_create-parallel_tool_calls" data-anchor="chat_create-parallel_tool_calls" id="chat_create-parallel_tool_calls-anchor" class="docs-markdown-content"><p>Constrains effort on reasoning for
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://platform.openai.com/docs/guides/reasoning" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">reasoning models</a>.
Currently supported values are <code>minimal</code>, <code>low</code>, <code>medium</code>, and <code>high</code>. Reducing
reasoning effort can result in faster responses and fewer tokens used
on reasoning in a response.</p>
<p>Note: The <code>gpt-5-pro</code> model defaults to (and only supports) <code>high</code> reasoning effort.</p></div></div></div><div class="param-row" id="chat_create-response_format" guide</a>.</p>

An older method of generating JSON responses.
Using <code>json_schema</code> is recommended for models that support it. Note that the
model will not generate JSON without a system or user message instructing it
to do so.</p></div></div><button class="param-expand-button" aria-expanded="true" aria-controls="chat_create-response_format-json_object_table"><span class="param-expand-chevron" null</p></div></div><div class="param-optl">Optional</div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>This feature is in Beta.
If specified, our system will make a best effort to sample deterministically, such that repeated requests with the same <code>seed</code> and parameters should return the same result.
Determinism is not guaranteed, and you should refer to the <code>system_fingerprint</code> response parameter to monitor changes in the backend.</p></div></div></div><div class="param-row" 9.29289Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a><div class="param-name">service_tier</div><div class="param-type"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>string</p></div></div><div class="param-optl">Optional</div><div class="param-default">Defaults to auto</div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>Specifies the processing type used for serving the request.</p>
<ul>
<li>If set to 'auto', then the request will be processed with the service tier configured in the Project settings. Unless otherwise configured, the Project will use 'default'.</li>
<li>If set to 'default', then the request will be processed with the standard pricing and performance for the selected model.</li>
<li>If set to '<a href="/docs/guides/flex-processing" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">flex</a>' or '<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://openai.com/api-priority-processing/" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">priority</a>', then the request will be processed with the corresponding service tier.</li>
<li>When not set, the default behavior is 'auto'.</li>
</ul>
<p>When the <code>service_tier</code> parameter is set, the response body will include the <code>service_tier</code> value based on the processing mode actually used to serve the request. This response value may be different from the value set in the parameter.</p></div></div></div><div class="param-row" id="chat_create-stop" data-normalized-id="chat-create-stop"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>boolean</p></div></div><div class="param-optl">Optional</div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>When true, stream obfuscation will be enabled. Stream obfuscation adds
random characters to an <code>obfuscation</code> field on streaming delta events to
normalize payload sizes as a mitigation to certain side-channel attacks.
These obfuscation fields are included by default, but add a small amount
of overhead to the data stream. You can set <code>include_obfuscation</code> to
false to optimize for bandwidth if you trust the network links between
your application and the OpenAI API.</p></div></div></div><div class="param-row" id="chat_create-stream_options-include_usage" data-normalized-id="chat-create-stream-options-include-usage"><div class="param-optl">Optional</div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>If set, an additional chunk will be streamed before the <code>data: [DONE]</code>
message. The <code>usage</code> field on this chunk shows the token usage statistics
for the entire request, and the <code>choices</code> field will always be an empty
array.</p>
<p>All other chunks will also include a <code>usage</code> field, but with a null
value. <strong>NOTE:</strong> If the stream is interrupted, you may not receive the
final usage chunk which contains the total token usage for the request.</p></div></div></div></div></div><div class="param-row" id="chat_create-temperature" class="param-optl">Optional</div><div class="param-default">Defaults to 1</div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>What sampling temperature to use, between 0 and 2. class="param-name">tool_choice</div><div class="param-type"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>string or object</p></div></div><div class="param-optl">Optional</div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>Controls which (if any) tool is called by the model.
<code>none</code> means the model will not call any tool and instead generates a message.
<code>auto</code> means the model can pick between generating a message or calling one or more tools.
<code>required</code> means the model must call one or more tools.
Specifying a particular tool via <code>{"type": "function", "function": {"name": "my_function"}}</code> forces the model to call that tool.</p>
<p><code>none</code> is the default when no tools are present. <code>auto</code> is the default if tools are present.</p></div></div><button class="param-expand-button" aria-expanded="true" class="param-reqd">Required</div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>Constrains the tools available to the model to a pre-defined set.</p>
<p><code>auto</code> allows the model to pick from among the allowed tools and generate a
message.</p>
<p><code>required</code> requires the model to call one or more of the allowed tools.</p></div></div></div><div class="param-row" id="chat_create-tool_choice-allowed_tools-allowed_tools-tools" mass. So 0.1 means only the tokens comprising the top 10% probability mass

</span><span>  },
</span><span><span>  </span><span class="hljs-attr">"service_tier"</span><span>: </span><span class="hljs-string">"default"</span><span>
</span></span><span>}</span></code></pre></div></div></div></div></div>

fill="currentColor"></path></svg></a><div class="param-name">service_tier</div><div class="param-type"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>string</p></div></div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>Specifies the processing type used for serving the request.</p>
<ul>
<li>If set to 'auto', then the request will be processed with the service tier configured in the Project settings. Unless otherwise configured, the Project will use 'default'.</li>
<li>If set to 'default', then the request will be processed with the standard pricing and performance for the selected model.</li>
<li>If set to '<a href="/docs/guides/flex-processing" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">flex</a>' or '<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://openai.com/api-priority-processing/" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">priority</a>', then the request will be processed with the corresponding service tier.</li>
<li>When not set, the default behavior is 'auto'.</li>
</ul>
<p>When the <code>service_tier</code> parameter is set, the response body will include the <code>service_tier</code> value based on the processing mode actually used to serve the request. This response value may be different from the value set in the parameter.</p></div></div></div><div class="param-row" id="chat-object-system_fingerprint" class="docs-markdown-content"><p>string</p></div></div></div><div class="param-desc"><div class="docs-markdown-content"><p>Specifies the processing type used for serving the request.</p>
<ul>
<li>If set to 'auto', then the request will be processed with the service tier configured in the Project settings. Unless otherwise configured, the Project will use 'default'.</li>
<li>If set to 'default', then the request will be processed with the standard pricing and performance for the selected model.</li>
<li>If set to '<a href="/docs/guides/flex-processing" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">flex</a>' or '<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://openai.com/api-priority-processing/" class="kZ98Q" data-underline="">priority</a>', then the request will be processed with the corresponding service tier.</li>
<li>When not set, the default behavior is 'auto'.</li>
</ul>
<p>When the <code>service_tier</code> parameter is set, the response body will include the <code>service_tier</code> value based on the processing mode actually used to serve the request. This response value may be different from the value set in the parameter.</p></div></div></div><div class="param-row" id="chat_streaming-streaming-system_fingerprint"
